< Review>
Please be aware of this place, maybe it's not bad for everyone, but it definitely was for me and half the other people who reviewed it. After having my car towed to Airport collision right after my accident, this was my experience.
Customer service: Grade D
The women at the front desk will tell you the most basic and generic answers to any question you have. If you ask when your car will be ready they will always give you the generic answer "2 weeks" when in reality your car is not being worked on & if you look at other reviews on here they will say the exact same. If you ask to speak to the owner Hiro, he's always "out".  If they say they will call you back, they won't! There was only one lady who called me back and she was very nice, but the rest of them are just sitting on pay roll reading from note cards, what it seems like. The only time I received any information that helped me was when I spoke to Hiro himself, he broke everything down and explained it.

Repair service: Grade D
When I went to see the progress of the car, I came to find out that whenever they moved my car they destroyed my rear diffuser that attached to the bottom of my rear bumper( my car had front end damage only, the rear was completely fine) & it was completely bent. They ended up bending it back, but that just let's you know they don't take every step to make sure they don't cause damage to customer vehicles.
When I finally got my car back after weeks of them saying it's going to be done on a particular day, my car a 07 BMW Was in limp mode which reduced the power of my car drastically. When I brought it to their attention they ran the codes and one was 30cf for my waistgate and they said they did not touch those components so I gave them the Benefit of the doubt because that part is apart of my turbo which should not have been touched. So I take it to my mechanic and he straight up tells me that whoever fixed my car did a sloppy job when it came to putting certain parts back, they also did not put my belly pan splash guard back so now there's nothing protecting my engine bay from road debris. My Mechanic plugged back in one of my vacuum lines that was not put back in and the code went straight away( job was so easy he didn't even charge me). Now keep in mind when I brought it back to Airport collision they did not even try to look underneath the hood, they ran the codes and decided they were not at fault and sent me on my way and assumed no responsibility. Also my driver side window controls did not work at all (not blaming them) however when I brought it to their attention they told me that they would order the part, after 2 weeks of waiting for this part I ended up getting it on my own & ive yet to be called..The paint came out very nice I must say and I didn't have gaps in the parts they replaced, but as a whole my experience was horrible, parts not being put back, damages that weren't there when I first brought the car, horrid customer service, them not being able to take responsibility when they made a mistake. What is done is done, all I can tell the next man is Yelp reviews do not lie, because i definitely looked at them before my car was repaired and everything everyone said was dead accurate. Excercise your options before you take it to this place, this play shouldn't even a last option, there are so many better collision repair centers to choose from. Stay away from this crooked place.< /Review>

<Review>I happened upon this Farmer's Market in the park today.

There are 2 designated entrances & exit.
Before entering you are politely asked to wash your hands at a very clean hand portable washing station.
Masks & distancing required.
X's on the ground helped to know how far to stand while in the market area.

1534698243749</date>
< text>
Smaller by far than the Sunday market under the freeway, but a good selection of vendors, including some esoteric small operations selling Hummus, Sourdough, Artesan Vinegars, Smoked Fish etc. There's enough F&V stalls to make it worth going and the extra stalls add some interest. 'Drunken Loaf' sell their bread there, which is the best in Sacramento. Also the lady selling the Salmon and Halibut - we love her smoked fish!
Ok, it's in 'Da Hood', but it's really nice going there. Mostly there is a musician playing and stalls with information on WIC, Jump Bikes, EBT and other things.
Parking isn't a problem, less oppressive than the Sunday market and you can be in and out in minutes.<//text>

This is a typical coin-op self-service car wash, however, this place is run down. There is graffiti around the area while the equipment is run down. Things to note:

+ Coin machine dispenses quarters, not tokens
-- Nozzle options are 'Soap' 'Foam Brush' and 'Spot Free Rinse'. The spot free rinse is just water, which includes many many water sports once you use it.
-- There is no wax options, nor a compressed-air drying option.

This place is very limited and isn't really worth it, unless you just need to spray mud off. Beyond that, go elsewhere.<//review>

< text>
So, been looking forward to review this place. Let me tell you why. I have been coming here for about two years at fist with a friend, who told me i had to check this place out.
Now you guys know, i keep it real and honest...... So here I go.
At first, it doesn't seem like much to look at. I mean its kind of dry and dead looking, on the outside and the Taco truck next to it kind of threw me off.
Oooh, but don't judge a book by it's cover really!!
Walking through the front gates you immediately enter an oasis with the standard old school gardners shack at front and center. They have a variety of cement and ceramic decor and a few things around the shack. What really got me is the selection of trees and different shrubs and roses, palms big and small there is allot. They even make there own potting soil and my plants thrive in it.

However the best part of coming here is picking Freddie's brain about plants and how to grow em and keep them alive. What's good for seasonal or all year round, i mean he is a wealth of information. Always friendly and professional and sticks with you till you are done. I've seen him many times interact with customers and honestly i can say I've never seen him walk away from one until they were done.

So all in all i highly recommend this place giving it a whole heartedüëçüëçüëçüëçüëçü§†....I would also like to add a special note of thanks to Freddie for donating all the plants and soil to help our church House of Refuge with restoring an elderly woman's garden, it was a great thing to see how happy she was. Made possible by his donations.< /text>

< text>
Ambiance :

Music was painfully loud and Im used to loud . They had a mariachi which I love but their speakers were blasting  to try to cover the music from their small bar in the next room. The bar was louder than any night club and it was just a very uncomfortable experience.  I walked out with a headache.

Food:

Mediocre .  They serves in big plates that are mainly 95% rice and beans.  The food is nothing  special and overpriced.  We had Shirmp al mojo de ajo and  it was undercooked and they used garlic seasoning instead of real garlic (8 small shrimps. I counted them). We ordered salad instead of rice and beans and don't have a single homemade dressing. The spicy  salsa was basically canned chipotle  chillies with some seasoning.  The bacon wrapped shrimp was okay... bacon was a little burned . The taquitos were okay and enchilada was just okay. Margaritas tasted like a lemonade kool-aid.

This place has so much potential the place it's really nice and  they have good menu but they lack  good chef and good management.<//text>

< text>
The best Mexican food. The lunch specials are cheap and very generous. Carnitas on Mondays only.

Since the interior of the building is domed, it must have been made with steel re-enforced concrete.

Concave ceilings aren't good for amplified music and loud crowds. So acoustics is bad and cell data service is weak.

When I eat there and there is live music, I eat in the patio. I get the same great service.< /text>
